        SELECT [c0].[Id], [c0].[CreaDate], [c0].[CreaUser], [c0].[Description], [c0].[IsDeleted], [c0].[IsStatus], [c0].[LoginCount], [c0].[ModDate], [c0].[ModUser], [c0].[Name], [c0].[OrderNo]

) AS [t3]

) AS [t]

    WHERE [c0].[IsDeleted] IS NULL

LEFT JOIN (

    FROM [ContentPage] AS [c2]
    WHERE [c2].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
